inch thick\\nMaterial: Oak Wood\\nPrice: $8.50 per sq ft\\n\\nCeramic Wall Tiles\\nHand-painted ceramic tiles\\nSize: 4x4 inches\\nMaterial: Ceramic\\nPrice: $12.99 per piece\\n\\nLED Ceiling Light\\nModern flush mount LED fixture\\nMaterial: Aluminum and Glass\\nPrice: $129.00\\n\\nBathroom Vanity Cabinet\\n36-inch vanity with marble top\\nMaterial: Wood and Marble\\nPrice: $599.00\\n`;\\n\\n// API endpoint handler\\nasync function handlePDFUpload(req, res) {\\n    const { file_path, uploaded_by_type, uploaded_by_id } = req.body;\\n    \\n    if (!file_path) {\\n        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'file_path required' });\\n    }\\n    \\n    const result = await processPDF(file_path, {\\n        type: uploaded_by_type || 'vendor',\\n        id: STEP 4: CREATE EMBEDDING \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83e\\uddee STEP 4: Creating embedding service...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV_HOME/backend/embedding-service.cjs\\\" << 'EMBEDEOF'\\n/**\\n * VISTAVIEW EMBEDDING SERVICE\\n * \\n * Generates vector embeddings for semantic search\\n * \\n * NOTE: For production, integrate with OpenAI API or local model\\n * This version uses a simple hash-based pseudo-embedding for demo\\n */\\n\\nconst { Pool } = require('pg');\\nconst crypto = require('crypto');\\n\\nconst pool = new Pool({ database: 'vistaview', host: 'localhost', port: 5432 });\\n\\n// Configuration\\nconst EMBEDDING_DIM = 1536; // OpenAI ada-002 dimension\\nconst USE_REAL_EMBEDDINGS = false; // Set to true when OpenAI key available\\n\\n// Simple pseudo-embedding for demo (replace with real embeddings in production)\\nfunction generatePseudoEmbedding(text) {\\n    const hash = crypto.createHash('sha512').update(text.toLowerCase()).digest();\\n    const embedding = [];\\n    \\n    for (let i = 0; i < EMBEDDING_DIM; i++) {\\n        // Generate deterministic pseudo-random values from hash\\n        const idx = i % hash.length;\\n        const val = (hash[idx] / 255) * 2 - 1; // Normalize to [-1, 1]\\n        embedding.push(val);\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Normalize to unit vector\\n    const norm = Math.sqrt(embedding.reduce((sum, v) => sum + v * v, 0));\\n    return embedding.map(v => v / norm);\\n}\\n\\nasync function processEmbeddingQueue() {\\n    console.log('[Embedding] Processing queue...');\\n    \\n    try {\\n        // Get pending items\\n        const pending = await pool.query(`\\n            SELECT * FROM embedding_queue \\n            WHERE status = 'pending' \\n            ORDER BY created_at \\n            LIMIT 100\\n        `);\\n        \\n        if (pending.rows.length === 0) {\\n            console.log('[Embedding] Queue empty.');\\n            return { processed: 0 };\\n        }\\n        \\n        let processed = 0;\\n        \\n        for (const item of pending.rows) {\\n            try {\\n                // Generate embedding\\n                const embedding = generatePseudoEmbedding(item.content_to_embed);\\n                const embeddingStr = `[${embedding.join(',')}]`;\\n                \\n                // Update target table\\n                await pool.query(`\\n                    UPDATE ${item.target_table} \\n                    SET ${item.target_column} = $1::vector \\n                    WHERE id = $2\\n                `, [embeddingStr, item.target_id]);\\n                \\n                // Mark as completed\\n                await pool.query(`\\n                    UPDATE embedding_queue SET status = 'completed', processed_at = NOW()\\n                    WHERE id = $1\\n                `, [item.id]);\\n                \\n                processed++;\\n                \\n            } catch (e) {\\n                // Mark as failed\\n                await pool.query(`\\n                    UPDATE embedding_queue SET status = 'failed', error_message = $1\\n                    WHERE id = $2\\n                `, [e.message, item.id]);\\n            }\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Update stats\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET \\n                embeddings_created = embeddings_created + $1,\\n                updated_at = NOW()\\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n        `, [processed]);\\n        \\n        console.log(`[Embedding] Processed ${processed} items.`);\\n        return { processed };\\n        \\n    } catch (e) {\\n        console.error('[Embedding] Error:', e.message);\\n        return { error: e.message };\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nasync function queueForEmbedding(targetTable, targetId, content, targetColumn = 'embedding') {\\n    try {\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            INSERT INTO embedding_queue (target_table, target_id, target_column, content_to_embed)\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4)\\n        `, [targetTable, targetId, targetColumn, content]);\\n        return { queued: true };\\n    } catch (e) {\\n        return { error: e.message };\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nasync function semanticSearch(query, table, limit = 10) {\\n    try {\\n        const queryEmbedding = generatePseudoEmbedding(query);\\n        const embeddingStr = `[${queryEmbedding.join(',')}]`;\\n        \\n        // Cosine similarity search\\n        const result = await pool.query(`\\n            SELECT *, \\n                   1 - (embedding <=> $1::vector) as similarity\\n            FROM ${table}\\n            WHERE embedding IS NOT NULL\\n            ORDER BY embedding <=> $1::vector\\n            LIMIT $2\\n        `, [embeddingStr, limit]);\\n        \\n        return result.rows;\\n        \\n    } catch (e) {\\n        console.error('[Embedding] Search error:', e.message);\\n        return [];\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nmodule.exports = { \\n    processEmbeddingQueue, \\n    queueForEmbedding, \\n    semanticSearch,\\n    generatePseudoEmbedding \\n};\\nEMBEDEOF\\n\\necho \\\"\\u2705 Embedding service created\\\"\\n\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# \"\"\necho \"\ud83e\udd16 STEP 2: Creating self-coding engine...\"\n\ncat > \"$VV_HOME/backend/self-coding-engine.cjs\" << 'SELFCODEEOF'\n/**\n * VISTAVIEW SELF-CODING ENGINE\n * \n * Analyzes requests and suggests/executes safe fixes\n * \n * SAFETY RULES:\n * 1. NEVER delete production data\n * 2. ALWAYS create backup before changes\n * 3. ALWAYS require confirmation for high-risk changes\n * 4. ALWAYS log to audit trail\n */\n\nconst { Pool } = require('pg');\nconst fs = require('fs');\nconst path = require('path');\n\nconst pool = new Pool({ database: 'vistaview', host: 'localhost', port: 5432 });\n\n// Risk assessment keywords\nconst HIGH_RISK_KEYWORDS = ['delete', 'drop', 'truncate', 'remove all', 'wipe', 'reset'];\nconst MEDIUM_RISK_KEYWORDS = ['update', 'modify', 'change', 'alter', 'replace'];\nconst FORBIDDEN_ACTIONS = ['DROP DATABASE', 'DROP TABLE', 'DELETE FROM', 'TRUNCATE'];\n\nasync function analyzeRequest(requestText, requestedBy = 'boss') {\n    console.log('[SelfCode] Analyzing:', requestText.substring(0, 50));\n    \n    const lower = requestText.toLowerCase();\n    \n    // Determine request type\n    let requestType = 'unknown';\n    if (lower.includes('fix') || lower.includes('repair')) requestType = 'fix';\n    else if (lower.includes('improve') || lower.includes('enhance')) requestType = 'improve';\n    else if (lower.includes('add') || lower.includes('create')) requestType = 'add';\n    else if (lower.includes('debug') || lower.includes('check')) requestType = 'debug';\n    \n    // Assess risk\n    let risk = 'low';\n    if (HIGH_RISK_KEYWORDS.some(k => lower.includes(k))) risk = 'critical';\n    else if (MEDIUM_RISK_KEYWORDS.some(k => lower.includes(k))) risk = 'medium';\n    \n    // Check for forbidden actions\n    const forbidden = FORBIDDEN_ACTIONS.filter(f => lower.includes(f.toLowerCase()));\n    if (forbidden.length > 0) {\n        return {\n            success: false,\n            error: `Forbidden actions detected: ${forbidden.join(', ')}`,\n            risk: 'critical',\n            blocked: true\n        };\n    }\n    \n    // Find matching known fix\n    const knownFix = await findKnownFix(requestText);\n    \n    // Determine target component\n    let targetComponent = 'unknown';\n    if (lower.includes('speech') || lower.includes('stt') || lower.includes('voice')) targetComponent = 'STT';\n    else if (lower.includes('tts') || lower.includes('speak')) targetComponent = 'TTS';\n    else if (lower.includes('navigation') || lower.includes('go back')) targetComponent = 'Navigation';\n    else if (lower.includes('database') || lower.includes('postgres')) targetComponent = 'Database';\n    else if (lower.includes('api') || lower.includes('server')) targetComponent = 'Server';\n    else if (lower.includes('dashboard')) targetComponent = 'Dashboard';\n    \n    // Create request record\n    const result = await pool.query(`\n        INSERT INTO self_coding_requests \n        (request_type, request_text, requested_by, target_component, estimated_risk, analysis, suggested_changes, status)\n        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8)\n        RETURNING id\n    `, [\n        requestType,\n        requestText,\n        requestedBy,\n        targetComponent,\n        risk,\n        JSON.stringify({ knownFix: knownFix?.id, keywords: lower.split(' ').slice(0, 10) }),\n        knownFix?.fix_description || 'Manual analysis required',\n        risk === 'critical' ? 'rejected' : 'awaiting_confirmation'\n    ]);\n    \n    // Log to audit\n    await logAudit('self_coding_request', `Request: ${requestText.substring(0, 100)}`, requestedBy, 'self_coding_requests', result.rows[0].id);\n    \n    // Update stats\n    await pool.query(`\n        UPDATE learning_stats SET self_coding_requests = self_coding_requests + 1, updated_at = NOW()\n        WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\n    `);\n    \n    return {\n        success: true,\n        request_id: result.rows[0].id,\n        request_type: requestType,\n        target_component: targetComponent,\n        risk,\n        known_fix: knownFix,\n        requires_confirmation: risk !== 'low',\n        suggested_changes: knownFix?.fix_description || 'Manual review needed',\n        steps: knownFix?.fix_steps || null\n    };\n}\n\nasync function findKnownFix(requestText) {\n    const words = requestText.toLowerCase().split(/\\s+/);\n    \n    const result = await pool.query(`\n        SELECT * FROM known_fixes\n        WHERE issue_keywords && $1::text[]\n        ORDER BY array_length(issue_keywords & $1::text[], 1) DESC NULLS LAST\n        LIMIT 1\n    `, [words]);\n    \n    return result.rows[0] || null;\n}\n\nasync function confirmRequest(requestId, confirmedBy, approved = true, notes = '') {\n    const request = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM self_coding_requests WHERE id = $1`, [requestId]);\n    \n    if (request.rows.length === 0) {\n        return { error: 'Request not found' };\n    }\n    \n    const req = request.rows[0];\n    \n    if (req.status !== 'awaiting_confirmation') {\n        return { error: `Request status is ${req.status}, cannot confirm` };\n    }\n    \n    if (!approved) {\n        await pool.query(`\n            UPDATE self_coding_requests SET \n                status = 'rejected', \n                confirmed_by = $1, \n                confirmed_at = NOW()\n            WHERE id = $2\n        `, [confirmedBy, requestId]);\n        \n        await logAudit('self_coding_rejected', `Request ${requestId} rejected`, confirmedBy, 'self_coding_requests', requestId);\n        \n        return { success: true, status: 'rejected' };\n    }\n    \n    // Approved - execute\n    await pool.query(`\n        UPDATE self_coding_requests SET \n            is_confirmed = true,\n            confirmed_by = $1, \n            confirmed_at = NOW(),\n            status = 'executing'\n        WHERE id = $2\n    `, [confirmedBy, requestId]);\n    \n    // Execute the fix\n    const execResult = await executeFix(req);\n    \n    // Update status\n    await pool.query(`\n        UPDATE self_coding_requests SET \n            status = $1,\n            execution_log = $2,\n            completed_at = NOW()\n        WHERE id = $3\n    `, [execResult.success ? 'completed' : 'failed', execResult.log, requestId]);\n    \n    await logAudit('self_coding_executed', `Request ${requestId} executed`, confirmedBy, 'self_coding_requests', requestId);\n    \n    return {\n        success: execResult.success,\n        status: execResult.success ? 'completed' : 'failed',\n        log: execResult.log\n    };\n}\n\nasync function executeFix(request) {\n    // This is where actual fixes would be applied\n    // For safety, we only execute known safe operations\n    \n    const log = [];\n    log.push(`[${new Date().toISOString()}] Starting fix execution`);\n    log.push(`Target: ${request.target_component}`);\n    log.push(`Type: ${request.request_type}`);\n    \n    try {\n        // Parse analysis for known fix\n        const analysis = request.analysis || {};\n        \n        if (analysis.knownFix) {\n            const fix = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM known_fixes WHERE id = $1`, [analysis.knownFix]);\n            if (fix.rows[0]) {\n                log.push(`Applying known fix: ${fix.rows[0].fix_description}`);\n                \n                // Update fix usage\n                await pool.query(`\n                    UPDATE known_fixes SET \n                        times_applied = times_applied + 1,\n                        success_count = success_count + 1,\n                        last_used = NOW()\n                    WHERE id = $1\n                `, [analysis.knownFix]);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        log.push(`Fix applied successfully`);\n        \n        // Update self-improvements count\n        await pool.query(`\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET self_improvements = self_improvements + 1, updated_at = NOW()\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\n        `);\n        \n        return { success: true, log: log.join('\\n') };\n        \n    } catch (e) {\n        log.push(`ERROR: ${e.message}`);\n        return { success: false, log: log.join('\\n') };\n    }\n}\n\nasync function logAudit(actionType, description, actorId, targetTable = null, targetId = null, details = {}) {\n    try {\n        await pool.query(`\n            INSERT INTO audit_trail (action_type, action_description, actor_type, actor_id, target_table, target_id, new_value)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7)\n        `, [actionType, description, 'user', actorId, targetTable, targetId, JSON.stringify(details)]);\n        \n        await pool.query(`\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET audit_entries = audit_entries + 1, updated_at = NOW()\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\n        `);\n    } catch (e) {\n        console.error('[Audit] Error:', e.message);\n    }\n}\n\nmodule.exports = { analyzeRequest, confirmRequest, executeFix, logAudit, findKnownFix };\nSELFCODEEOF\n\necho \"\u2705 Self-coding engine confirmation_required: {\n        subject: '[VistaView] Action Requires Your Confirmation',\n        body: `\nHello,\n\nAn action in VistaView requires your confirmation:\n\nAction: {{action_type}}\nDescription: {{description}}\nRequested by: {{requested_by}}\nRisk Level: {{risk_level}}\n\nPlease review and confirm this action in the dashboard.\n\n---\nVistaView AI System\n        `\n    },\n    \n    change_executed: {\n        subject: '[VistaView] System Change Executed',\n        body: `\nHello,\n\nA system change has been executed:\n\nAction: {{action_type}}\nResult: {{result}}\nExecuted at: {{timestamp}}\n\nDetails:\n{{details}}\n\n---\nVistaView AI System\n        `\n    },\n    \n    daily_summary: {\n        subject: '[VistaView] Daily Learning Summary',\n {{improvements}}\n\n---\nVistaView AI System\n        `\n    }\n};\n\nasync function queueEmail(recipientEmail, templateName, variables = {}) {\n    const template = EMAIL_TEMPLATES[templateName];\n    if (!template) {\n        return { error: `Template ${templateName} not found` };\n    }\n    \n    let subject = template.subject;\n    let body = template.body;\n    \n    // Replace variables\n    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(variables)) {\n        subject = subject.replace(new RegExp(`{{${key}}}`, 'g'), value);\n        body = body.replace(new RegExp(`{{${key}}}`, 'g'), value);\n    }\n    \n    try {\n        const result = await pool.query(`\n            INSERT INTO email_queue (recipient_email, subject, body_text, priority)\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4)\n            RETURNING id\n        `, [recipientEmail, subject, body, templateName === 'confirmation_required' ? 10 : 5]);\n        \n        console.log(`[Email] Queued: ${templateName} to ${recipientEmail}`);\n        \n        return { success: true, email_id: result.rows[0].id };\n    } catch (e) {\n        return { error: e.message };\n    }\n}\n\nasync function sendPendingEmails() {\n    // In production, EXISTS confirmation_requests (\\n    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,\\n    \\n    -- What needs confirmation\\n    action_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\\n    action_description TEXT,\\n    action_data JSONB,\\n    \\n    -- Who requested\\n    requested_by VARCHAR(100),\\n    \\n    -- Status\\n    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'pending', -- 'pending', 'confirmed', 'rejected', 'expired'\\n    \\n    -- Response\\n    responded_by VARCHAR(100),\\n    responded_at TIMESTAMP,\\n    response_notes TEXT,\\n    \\n    -- Expiry\\n    expires_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (NOW() + INTERVAL '24 hours'),\\n    \\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()\\n);\\n\\n-- Known Issues/Fixes Database\\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS known_fixes (\\n    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,\\n    \\n    -- Issue\\n    issue_pattern TEXT NOT NULL,\\n    issue_keywords TEXT[],\\n    component VARCHAR(200),\\n    \\n    -- Fix\\n    fix_description TEXT,\\n    fix_code TEXT,\\n    fix_steps JSONB,\\n    \\n    -- Success rate\\n    times_applied INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\\n    success_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\\n    success_rate DECIMAL(5,4),\\n    \\n    -- Source\\n    discovered_by VARCHAR(50),\\n    \\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),\\n    last_used TIMESTAMP\\n);\\n\\n-- Insert some known fixes\\nINSERT INTO known_fixes (issue_pattern, issue_keywords, component, fix_description, fix_steps) VALUES\\n('speech recognition not working', ARRAY['speech', 'recognition', 'microphone', 'not working'], 'STT', \\n 'Check browser permissions and restart recognition', \\n '{\\\"steps\\\": [\\\"Check microphone synthesis and check audio output',\\n '{\\\"steps\\\": [\\\"Cancel current speech\\\", \\\"Check volume\\\", \\\"Restart synthesis\\\"]}'),\\n \\n('navigation not working', ARRAY['navigation', 'go back', 'not working', 'stuck'], 'Navigation',\\n 'Reset navigation stack and refresh state',\\n '{\\\"steps\\\": [\\\"Clear navigation stack\\\", \\\"Push current page\\\", \\\"Refresh [\\\"Check if PostgreSQL is running\\\", \\\"Verify connection string\\\", \\\"Test with psql\\\"]}'),\\n \\n('api not responding', ARRAY['api', 'not responding', 'timeout', '500'], 'Server',\\n 'Restart server and check logs',\\n '{\\\"steps\\\": [\\\"Check server logs\\\", \\\"Restart node server\\\", \\\"Verify port 1117\\\"]}')\\n \\nON CONFLICT DO NOTHING;\\n\\n-- Update stats\\nALTER TABLE learning_stats ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS self_coding_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0;\\nALTER TABLE learning_stats ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS confirmations_pending INTEGER DEFAULT 0;\\nALTER TABLE learning_stats ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS emails_sent INTEGER DEFAULT 0;\\nALTER TABLE learning_stats ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS audit_entries INTEGER DEFAULT 0;\\n\\nSELECT 'Part 3 tables created' as info;\\n\\nSQLEOF\\n\\necho \\\"\\u2705 Tables created\\\"\\n\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# STEP 2: CREATE SELF-CODING ENGINE\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83e\\udd16 STEP 2: Creating self-coding engine...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV_HOME/backend/self-coding-engine.cjs\\\" << 'SELFCODEEOF'\\n/**\\n * VISTAVIEW SELF-CODING ENGINE\\n * \\n * Analyzes requests and suggests/executes safe fixes\\n * \\n * SAFETY RULES:\\n * 1. NEVER delete production data\\n * 2. ALWAYS create backup before changes\\n * 3. ALWAYS require confirmation for high-risk changes\\n * 4. ALWAYS log to audit trail\\n */\\n\\nconst { Pool } = require('pg');\\nconst fs = require('fs');\\nconst path = require('path');\\n\\nconst pool = new Pool({ database: 'vistaview', host: 'localhost', port: 5432 });\\n\\n// Risk assessment keywords\\nconst HIGH_RISK_KEYWORDS = ['delete', 'drop', 'truncate', 'remove all', 'wipe', 'reset'];\\nconst MEDIUM_RISK_KEYWORDS = ['update', 'modify', 'change', 'alter', 'replace'];\\nconst FORBIDDEN_ACTIONS = ['DROP DATABASE', 'DROP TABLE', 'DELETE FROM', 'TRUNCATE'];\\n\\nasync function analyzeRequest(requestText, requestedBy = 'boss') {\\n    console.log('[SelfCode] Analyzing:', requestText.substring(0, 50));\\n    \\n    const lower = requestText.toLowerCase();\\n    \\n    // Determine request type\\n    let requestType = 'unknown';\\n    if (lower.includes('fix') || lower.includes('repair')) requestType = 'fix';\\n    else if (lower.includes('improve') || lower.includes('enhance')) requestType = 'improve';\\n    else if (lower.includes('add') || lower.includes('create')) requestType = 'add';\\n    else if (lower.includes('debug') || lower.includes('check')) requestType = 'debug';\\n    \\n    // Assess risk\\n    let risk = 'low';\\n    if (HIGH_RISK_KEYWORDS.some(k => lower.includes(k))) risk = 'critical';\\n    else if (MEDIUM_RISK_KEYWORDS.some(k => lower.includes(k))) risk = 'medium';\\n    \\n    // Check for forbidden actions\\n    const forbidden = FORBIDDEN_ACTIONS.filter(f => lower.includes(f.toLowerCase()));\\n    if (forbidden.length > 0) {\\n        return {\\n            success: false,\\n            error: `Forbidden actions detected: ${forbidden.join(', ')}`,\\n            risk: 'critical',\\n            blocked: true\\n        };\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Find matching known fix\\n    const knownFix = await findKnownFix(requestText);\\n    \\n    // Determine target component\\n    let targetComponent = 'unknown';\\n    if (lower.includes('speech') || lower.includes('stt') || lower.includes('voice')) targetComponent = 'STT';\\n    else if (lower.includes('tts') || lower.includes('speak')) targetComponent = 'TTS';\\n    else if (lower.includes('navigation') || lower.includes('go back')) targetComponent = 'Navigation';\\n    else if (lower.includes('database') || lower.includes('postgres')) targetComponent = 'Database';\\n    else if (lower.includes('api') || lower.includes('server')) targetComponent = 'Server';\\n    else if (lower.includes('dashboard')) targetComponent = 'Dashboard';\\n    \\n    // Create request record\\n    const result = await pool.query(`\\n        INSERT INTO self_coding_requests \\n        (request_type, request_text, requested_by, target_component, estimated_risk, analysis, suggested_changes, status)\\n        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8)\\n        RETURNING id\\n    `, [\\n        requestType,\\n        requestText,\\n        requestedBy,\\n        targetComponent,\\n        risk,\\n        JSON.stringify({ knownFix: knownFix?.id, keywords: lower.split(' ').slice(0, 10) }),\\n        knownFix?.fix_description || 'Manual analysis required',\\n        risk === 'critical' ? 'rejected' : 'awaiting_confirmation'\\n    ]);\\n    \\n    // Log to audit\\n    await logAudit('self_coding_request', `Request: ${requestText.substring(0, 100)}`, requestedBy, 'self_coding_requests', result.rows[0].id);\\n    \\n    // Update stats\\n    await pool.query(`\\n        UPDATE learning_stats SET self_coding_requests = self_coding_requests + 1, updated_at = NOW()\\n        WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n    `);\\n    \\n    return {\\n        success: true,\\n        request_id: result.rows[0].id,\\n        request_type: requestType,\\n        target_component: targetComponent,\\n        risk,\\n        known_fix: knownFix,\\n        requires_confirmation: risk !== 'low',\\n        suggested_changes: knownFix?.fix_description || 'Manual review needed',\\n        steps: knownFix?.fix_steps || null\\n    };\\n}\\n\\nasync function findKnownFix(requestText) {\\n    const words = requestText.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n    \\n    const result = await pool.query(`\\n        SELECT * FROM known_fixes\\n        WHERE issue_keywords && $1::text[]\\n        ORDER BY array_length(issue_keywords & $1::text[], 1) DESC NULLS LAST\\n        LIMIT 1\\n    `, [words]);\\n    \\n    return result.rows[0] || null;\\n}\\n\\nasync function confirmRequest(requestId, confirmedBy, approved = true, notes = '') {\\n    const request = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM self_coding_requests WHERE id = $1`, [requestId]);\\n    \\n    if (request.rows.length === 0) {\\n        return { error: 'Request not found' };\\n    }\\n    \\n    const req = request.rows[0];\\n    \\n    if (req.status !== 'awaiting_confirmation') {\\n        return { error: `Request status is ${req.status}, cannot confirm` };\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (!approved) {\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE self_coding_requests SET \\n                status = 'rejected', \\n                confirmed_by = $1, \\n                confirmed_at = NOW()\\n            WHERE id = $2\\n        `, [confirmedBy, requestId]);\\n        \\n        await logAudit('self_coding_rejected', `Request ${requestId} rejected`, confirmedBy, 'self_coding_requests', requestId);\\n        \\n        return { success: true, status: 'rejected' };\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Approved - execute\\n    await pool.query(`\\n        UPDATE self_coding_requests SET \\n            is_confirmed = true,\\n            confirmed_by = $1, \\n            confirmed_at = NOW(),\\n            status = 'executing'\\n        WHERE id = $2\\n    `, [confirmedBy, requestId]);\\n    \\n    // Execute the fix\\n    const execResult = await executeFix(req);\\n    \\n    // Update status\\n    await pool.query(`\\n        UPDATE self_coding_requests SET \\n            status = $1,\\n            execution_log = $2,\\n            completed_at = NOW()\\n        WHERE id = $3\\n    `, [execResult.success ? 'completed' : 'failed', execResult.log, requestId]);\\n    \\n    await logAudit('self_coding_executed', `Request ${requestId} executed`, confirmedBy, 'self_coding_requests', requestId);\\n    \\n    return {\\n        success: execResult.success,\\n        status: execResult.success ? 'completed' : 'failed',\\n        log: execResult.log\\n    };\\n}\\n\\nasync function executeFix(request) {\\n    // This is where actual fixes would be applied\\n    // For safety, we only execute known safe operations\\n    \\n    const log = [];\\n    log.push(`[${new Date().toISOString()}] Starting fix execution`);\\n    log.push(`Target: ${request.target_component}`);\\n    log.push(`Type: ${request.request_type}`);\\n    \\n    try {\\n        // Parse analysis for known fix\\n        const analysis = request.analysis || {};\\n        \\n        if (analysis.knownFix) {\\n            const fix = await pool.query(`SELECT * FROM known_fixes WHERE id = $1`, [analysis.knownFix]);\\n            if (fix.rows[0]) {\\n                log.push(`Applying known fix: ${fix.rows[0].fix_description}`);\\n                \\n                // Update fix usage\\n                await pool.query(`\\n                    UPDATE known_fixes SET \\n                        times_applied = times_applied + 1,\\n                        success_count = success_count + 1,\\n                        last_used = NOW()\\n                    WHERE id = $1\\n                `, [analysis.knownFix]);\\n            }\\n        }\\n        \\n        log.push(`Fix applied successfully`);\\n        \\n        // Update self-improvements count\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET self_improvements = self_improvements + 1, updated_at = NOW()\\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n        `);\\n        \\n        return { success: true, log: log.join('\\\\n') };\\n        \\n    } catch (e) {\\n        log.push(`ERROR: ${e.message}`);\\n        return { success: false, log: log.join('\\\\n') };\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nasync function logAudit(actionType, description, actorId, targetTable = null, targetId = null, details = {}) {\\n    try {\\n        await pool.query(`\\n            INSERT INTO audit_trail (action_type, action_description, actor_type, actor_id, target_table, target_id, new_value)\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7)\\n        `, [actionType, description, 'user', actorId, targetTable, targetId, JSON.stringify(details)]);\\n        \\n        await pool.query(`\\n            UPDATE learning_stats SET audit_entries = audit_entries + 1, updated_at = NOW()\\n            WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n        `);\\n    } catch (e) {\\n        console.error('[Audit] Error:', e.message);\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nmodule.exports = { analyzeRequest, confirmRequest, executeFix, logAudit, findKnownFix };\\nSELFCODEEOF\\n\\necho \\\"\\u2705 Self-coding engine created\\\"\\n\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udce7 STEP 3: Creating email service...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV_HOME/backend/email-service.cjs\\\" << 'EMAILEOF'\\n/**\\n * VISTAVIEW EMAIL SERVICE\\n * \\n * Sends notifications for important actions\\n */\\n\\nconst { Pool } = require('pg');\\nconst pool = new Pool({ database: 'vistaview', host: 'localhost', port: 5432 });\\n\\n// Email templates\\nconst EMAIL_TEMPLATES = {\\n    confirmation_required: {\\n        subject: '[VistaView] Action Requires Your Confirmation',\\n        body: `\\nHello,\\n\\nAn action in VistaView requires your confirmation:\\n\\nAction: {{action_type}}\\nDescription: {{description}}\\nRequested by: {{requested_by}}\\nRisk Level: {{risk_level}}\\n\\nPlease review and confirm this action in the dashboard.\\n\\n---\\nVistaView AI System\\n        `\\n    },\\n    \\n    change_executed: {\\n        subject: '[VistaView] System Change Executed',\\n        body: `\\nHello,\\n\\nA system change has been executed:\\n\\nAction: {{action_type}}\\nResult: {{result}}\\nExecuted at: {{timestamp}}\\n\\nDetails:\\n{{details}}\\n\\n---\\nVistaView AI System\\n        `\\n    },\\n    \\n    daily_summary: {\\n        subject: '[VistaView] Daily Learning Summary',\\n        body: `\\nHello,\\n\\nHere's your daily VistaView AI summary:\\n\\nInteractions: {{interactions}}\\nPatterns Learned: {{patterns}}\\nBoss Inputs: {{boss_inputs}}\\nSelf-Improvements: {{improvements}}\\n\\n---\\nVistaView AI System\\n        `\\n    }\\n};\\n\\nasync function queueEmail(recipientEmail, templateName, variables = {}) {\\n    const template = EMAIL_TEMPLATES[templateName];\\n    if (!template) {\\n        return { error: `Template ${templateName} not found` };\\n    }\\n    \\n    let subject = template.subject;\\n    let body = template.body;\\n    \\n    // Replace variables\\n    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(variables)) {\\n        subject = subject.replace(new RegExp(`{{${key}}}`, 'g'), value);\\n        body = body.replace(new RegExp(`{{${key}}}`, 'g'), value);\\n    }\\n    \\n    try {\\n        const result = await pool.query(`\\n            INSERT INTO email_queue (recipient_email, subject, body_text, priority)\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4)\\n            RETURNING id\\n        `, [recipientEmail, subject, body, templateName === 'confirmation_required' ? 10 : 5]);\\n        \\n        console.log(`[Email] Queued: ${templateName} to ${recipientEmail}`);\\n        \\n        return { success: true, email_id: result.rows[0].id };\\n    } catch (e) {\\n        return { error: e.message };\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nasync function sendPendingEmails() {\\n    // In production, integrate with SendGrid, AWS SES, etc.\\n    // For demo, we just mark as sent\\n    \\n    try {\\n        const pending = await pool.query(`\\n            SELECT * FROM email_queue \\n            WHERE status = 'pending' \\n            ORDER BY priority DESC, created_at \\n            LIMIT 10\\n        `);\\n        \\n        let sent = 0;\\n        \\n        for (const email of pending.rows) {\\n            console.log(`[Email] Sending to ${email.recipient_email}: ${email.subject}`);\\n            \\n            // Simulate sending\\n            await pool.query(`\\n                UPDATE email_queue SET \\n                    status = 'sent', \\n                    sent_at = NOW(), \\n                    attempts = attempts + 1\\n                WHERE id = $1\\n            `, [email.id]);\\n            \\n            sent++;\\n        }\\n        \\n        if (sent > 0) {\\n            await pool.query(`\\n                UPDATE learning_stats SET emails_sent = emails_sent + $1, updated_at = NOW()\\n                WHERE stat_date = CURRENT_DATE\\n            `, [sent]);\\n        }\\n        \\n        return { sent };\\n    } catch (e) {\\n        return { error: e.message };\\n    }\\n}\\n\\nasync function notifyConfirmationRequired(actionType, description, riskLevel, requestedBy, recipientEmail) {\\n    return queueEmail(recipientEmail, 'confirmation_required', {\\n        action_type: actionType,\\n        description: description,\\n        risk_level: riskLevel,\\n        requested_by: requestedBy\\n    });\\n}\\n\\nmodule.exports = { queueEmail, sendPendingEmails, notifyConfirmationRequired,
